\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00186}00186\ \ \ \ \ exponent\_range\ =\ numpy.arange(order\ +\ 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00187}00187\ \ \ \ \ sigma2\ =\ sigma\ *\ sigma}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00188}00188\ \ \ \ \ x\ =\ numpy.arange(-\/radius,\ radius+1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00189}00189\ \ \ \ \ phi\_x\ =\ numpy.exp(-\/0.5\ /\ sigma2\ *\ x\ **\ 2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00190}00190\ \ \ \ \ phi\_x\ =\ phi\_x\ /\ phi\_x.sum()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00191}00191\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00193}00193\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ phi\_x}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00194}00194\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00195}00195\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ f(x)\ =\ q(x)\ *\ phi(x)\ =\ q(x)\ *\ exp(p(x))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00196}00196\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ f'(x)\ =\ (q'(x)\ +\ q(x)\ *\ p'(x))\ *\ phi(x)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00201}00201\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ q[0]\ =\ 1}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00438}00438\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ This\ function\ computes\ the\ axis-\/specific\ Sobel\ gradient.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00439}00439\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ horizontal\ edges\ can\ emphasised\ with\ the\ horizontal\ trasform\ (axis=0),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00440}00440\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ the\ vertical\ edges\ with\ the\ vertical\ transform\ (axis=1)\ and\ so\ on\ for\ higher}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00441}00441\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ dimensions.\ These\ can\ be\ combined\ to\ give\ the\ magnitude.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00442}00442\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00445}00445\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ >>>\ from\ scipy\ import\ ndimage,\ datasets}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00446}00446\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ >>>\ import\ matplotlib.pyplot\ as\ plt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00447}00447\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ >>>\ import\ numpy\ as\ np}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00448}00448\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ >>>\ ascent\ =\ datasets.ascent().astype('int32')}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00449}00449\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ >>>\ sobel\_h\ =\ ndimage.sobel(ascent,\ 0)\ \ \#\ horizontal\ gradient}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00450}00450\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ >>>\ sobel\_v\ =\ ndimage.sobel(ascent,\ 1)\ \ \#\ vertical\ gradient}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00451}00451\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ >>>\ magnitude\ =\ np.sqrt(sobel\_h**2\ +\ sobel\_v**2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00452}00452\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ >>>\ magnitude\ *=\ 255.0\ /\ np.max(magnitude)\ \ \#\ normalization}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__filters_8py_source_l00453}00453\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ >>>\ fig,\ axs\ =\ plt.subplots(2,\ 2,\ figsize=(8,\ 8))}}
